09/09/2022, 20:55 - Arpit: #include <iostream>
using namespace std; 

int checkSum(int arr[],int n){
    int maxm=0; 
    for(int i=0; i<=n; i++){
        if(arr[i]<100){
            maxm=max(arr[i],maxm);
        }
    }
    return maxm;

}

int main(){

    int arr[10000];
    int n=0;
    int i=0;
    while(n!=-1){
        cin>>n;
        arr[i]=n;
        i++;
    }
    cout<<checkSum(arr, i);
    return 0;
}

Currently, processArray does not modify the array. You have to change this program so that any sequence of two or more consecutive two-digit numbers in the array are removed from the array and replaced with the smallest number from that sequence. The processArray method should modify the array in-place (preferably without creating a new array), and it should return the new length of the modified array.

For example, if these numbers were provided on the standard input:

3
26
32
612
121
61
23
38

6

Then the program should print:

3
26
612
121
23
661
6
Specifically, from the sequence 26, 32, only 26 is retained because it is the least number of that sequence, and from the sequence 61, 23, 38, only 23 is retained.

public class MyClass {
    
  
    public static void main(String args[]) {
      
      int ans = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
      boolean flag = true;
      while(flag==true){
          int in = sc.nextInt();
          if(in < 0){flag = false; continue;}
           list.add(in);
      }
      for(int e : list){
        //   System.out.println(e+" ");
          if(e < 100){
              ans = Math.max(ans,e);
          }
      }
      System.out.println(ans);
    }
    
}

10/09/2022, 00:07 - Aniwesh: import java.util.*;
public class MyClass {
    public static boolean isTwoDigit(int n){
    String s = ""+n;
    return s.length() == 2;
}
public static void main(String[] args) {

		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
      boolean flag = true;
      while(flag==true){
          int in = sc.nextInt();
          if(in < 0){flag = false; continue;}
           list.add(in);
      }
      int[] arr = new int[list.size()];
      for(int i=0; i<list.size();i++){
          arr[i] = list.get(i);
      }

		int twoDigitCounter = 0;
		int val = 0;
		int i = 0;
		int length = arr.length;
		while(true) {

			if(i == length) {
				break;
			}
// 			System.out.println(isTwoDigit(arr[i]));
			if(isTwoDigit(arr[i])) {
				twoDigitCounter++;
				
				if(twoDigitCounter == 2) {
					if(arr[i] < val ) {
						val = arr[i];
					}
					twoDigitCounter = 0;
					arr[--i] = val;
					length = length-1;
					arr = processArray(arr, i+1);
					val = 0;
				}
				else {
					val = arr[i];
					i++;
				}
			}
			else{
				i++;
				val = 0;
				twoDigitCounter = 0;
			}

		}
		for(int j = 0 ; j<length ; j++) {
			System.out.println(arr[j]);
		}
	}
	public static int[] processArray(int[] arr, int i) {

		for(int k = i; k<arr.length-1 ; k++) {

			arr[k] = arr[k+1];

		}
		return arr;


	}
}

10/09/2022, 00:22 - KHUSH Vit: import java.util.*;
public class Main {
    public static boolean isTwoDigit(int n){
    String s = ""+n;
    return s.length() == 2;
    }
    public static void main(String[] args) {

		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
        boolean flag = true;
        while(flag==true){
            int in = sc.nextInt();
            if(in < 0){flag = false; continue;}
             list.add(in);
        }
        int[] arr = new int[list.size()];
         for(int i=0; i<list.size();i++){
             arr[i] = list.get(i);
        }

		int twoDigitCounter = 0;
		int val = 0;
		int i = 0;
		int length = arr.length;
		while(true) {

			if(i == length) {
				break;
			}
// 			System.out.println(isTwoDigit(arr[i]));
			if(isTwoDigit(arr[i])) {
				twoDigitCounter++;
				
				if(twoDigitCounter == 2) {
					if(arr[i] < val ) {
						val = arr[i];
					}
					twoDigitCounter = 0;
					arr[--i] = val;
					length = length-1;
					arr = processArray(arr, i+1);
					val = 0;
				}
				else {
					val = arr[i];
					i++;
				}
			}
			else{
				i++;
				val = 0;
				twoDigitCounter = 0;
			}

		}
		for(int j = 0 ; j<length ; j++) {
			System.out.println(arr[j]);
		}
	}
	public static int[] processArray(int[] arr, int i) {

		for(int k = i; k<arr.length-1 ; k++) {

			arr[k] = arr[k+1];

		}
		return arr;


	}
}

Consider the following SQL query that will be used with an RDBMS:

SELECT Customer.Name 
FROM Customer, Store
WHERE Customer.StoreID = Store.ID
AND Customer.Age > 30
AND Store.Location = 'NCR'
Assume that ID is a primary key of the table Store. Which of the following statements are likely to be true?

Pick all that apply
In most cases, this query is likely to get faster if an index is built on the Location column of the Store table.
If there is an index on both the Customer.Age column and the Store.Location column, the database will be forced to choose which index to use to fetch matching rows, since it cannot use both.
If this query is submitted to the database, it will automatically build an index on the Location column of the Store table.
If the database has an index on the Store.Location column, but no index on the Customer.Age column, then the database is guaranteed to first use the index to fetch all Store rows with Location = 'NCR' and then fetch the matching Customer rows
If the database has does not have an index on the Location column of the Store table, then the database is guaranteed to first fetch rows of the Customer table with Age > 30 and then join those with matching Store rows.

10/09/2022, 01:20 - Aniwesh: import java.util.*;
public class MyClass {
    
  
    public static void main(String args[]) {
      
      int ans = Integer.MIN_VALUE;
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
      ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
      boolean flag = true;
      while(flag==true){
          int in = sc.nextInt();
          if(in < 0){flag = false; continue;}
           list.add(in);
      }
      for(int e : list){
        //   System.out.println(e+" ");
          if(e < 100){
              ans = Math.max(ans,e);
          }
      }
      System.out.println(ans);
    }
    
}

10/09/2022, 01:27 - AryanğŸŒš Vit: ote that the sequence 3, 35 has been replaced by 2 and the sequence 61, 29, 375 has been replaced by 3.

here is my code:

import java.util.*;
import java.io.*;

public class Main {
    public static int processArray(ArrayList<Integer> array) {
        ListIterator<Integer>iterator=array.listIterator();
        while (iterator.hasNext()) {
            Integer integer = (Integer) iterator.next();
            int count=0;
            if (integer%2!=0) {
                count=count++;
                iterator.remove();
                continue;
            }
            if(integer==-1)
                break;
            else
                iterator.previous();
            iterator.add(count);
            iterator.next();


        }

        return array.size();
    }

    public static void main (String[] args) {
        ArrayList<Integer> arrayList = new ArrayList<Integer>();
        Scanner in = new Scanner(System.in);
        while(in.hasNextInt()) {
            int num = in.nextInt();
            if (num < 0) 
                break;
            arrayList.add(new Integer(num));
        }
        int new_length = processArray(arrayList);
        for(int i=0; i<new_length; i++)
            System.out.println(arrayList.get(i));
    }
}

10/09/2022, 01:31 - Aniwesh: include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
    vector<int>v;// to store numbers
    int num;
    cin>>num;
    while(num!=-1)// while input is not -1
    {
        v.push_back(num);
        cin>>num;
    }
    stack<pair<int,int>>s;// to store number of digits and number
    int i=0;
    while(i<v.size())
    {
        int a=v[i],counter=0;
        while(a!=0)// count number of digits
        {
            counter++;
            a/=10;
        }
        if(counter==3)// if digits are 3
        {
            if(!s.empty() && s.top().first==3)// if previous no was of digits 3
            {
                if(s.top().second<v[i])
                {// check number is bigger or smaller
                    s.pop();
                    s.push({counter,v[i]});
                    v.erase(v.begin()+(i-1));// delete that number
                }
                else
                {
                    v.erase(v.begin()+i);// delete current number
                }
            }
            else
            {
                s.push({counter,v[i]});
                i++;
            }
        }
        else
        {
            s.push({counter,v[i]});
            i++;
        }
    }
    for(int i=0;i<v.size();i++)
    cout<<v[i]<<endl;// print modified array
    return 0;
}

Question

QUESTION 14
GROUP Coding SECTION Language Coding
14
Bob, a wildlife photographer, is going on a one day jungle tour 

 

Hire
Instructions
DOPOLEONISTA
00:40:19
The output should contain X, the maximum number of animals that can be clicked
Sample

 

Explanation 2:
In this example, the tour runs for 6 hours, and Bob can click pictures for 5 consecutive hours. The maximum nu

 

Complete the Program Fast in Java.


Answer

Total answers posted by the expert is: 1147

Code:

package demos;

import java.util.Scanner;

public class TestClass {
   public static int maxAnimakCapture(int[] a,int n, int k)
   {
       int max=0;
       if(n>k)
       {
           for(int i=0;i<=n-k;i++)
           {
               int tempmax = 0;
               for(int j=i;j<i+k;j++)
                   tempmax = tempmax + a[j];
               if(tempmax>max)
                   max = tempmax;
           }
       }
       else
       {
           for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
               max = max+a[i];
       }
       return max;
   }
   public static void main(String args[])
   {
       Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
       int n = sc.nextInt();
       int k = sc.nextInt();
       int a[] = new int[n];
       for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
           a[i] = sc.nextInt();
       System.out.println(maxAnimakCapture(a,n,k));
   }
}

Explanation:

public static int maxAnimakCapture(int[] a,int n, int k)
    {
        int max=0;
        //This checks if n is greater than k
        //if n is less then we need to check for n-k
        //that is if n=5 and k=3, we need to check for 3 subsets
        //like n=5, k=3, a = [1 2 3 4 5]
        //the subsets will be 1 2 3, 2 3 4, 3 4 5
        //so total subsets = n-k, since we start i from 0 we use i<=n-k
        //next we take k no of element starting from i and sum them(in j loop)
        if(n>k)
        {
            for(int i=0;i<=n-k;i++)
            {
                int tempmax = 0;
                for(int j=i;j<i+k;j++)
                    tempmax = tempmax + a[j];
                //checks if current tempmax is greater than preset max
                //if tempmax is greater then max = tempmax
                if(tempmax>max)
                    max = tempmax;
            }
        }
        //If n is greater than equal to k then
        //All the pictures can be taken so we add the complete array
        else
        {
            for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
                max = max+a[i];
        }
        return max;
    }

11/01/2023, 23:06 - AryanğŸŒš Vit: Kal 12.30 test 3
11/01/2023, 23:06 - Akhil Vit: import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.Scanner;

class Recruitment implements Comparable<Recruitment> {
    String name, qual, gender;
    int exp;
    public Recruitment(String name, String qual, int exp, String gender) {
        this.name = name;
        this.qual = qual;
        this.exp = exp;
        this.gender = gender;
    }

    public int compareTo(Recruitment o) {
        return this.exp - o.exp;
    }

    public String toString() {
        return this.name + " " + this.qual + " " + this.exp + " " + this.gender;
    }
}

public class Main {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        int n = sc.nextInt();
        ArrayList<Recruitment> recruits = new ArrayList<Recruitment>();
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            String name = sc.next();
            String qual = sc.next();
            int exp = sc.nextInt();
            String gender = sc.next();
            recruits.add(new Recruitment(name, qual, exp, gender));
        }
        Collections.sort(recruits);
        for (Recruitment recruit : recruits) {
            System.out.println(recruit);
        }
    }
}

09/02/2023, 08:48 - Prasoon Gujjar Vit: textFieldChanged() - This function is called when the value of the text field changes. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
textFieldFocused() - This function is called when the text field is focused. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
textFieldBlurred() - This function is called when the text field loses focus. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
buttonClicked() - This function is called when the button is clicked. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
mouseHovered() - This function is called when the mouse moves over the text. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
mouseLeft() - This function is called when the mouse moves away from the text. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
keyPressed() - This function is called when a key is pressed within the text area. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
onload - This event is triggered when the page is fully loaded. It displays an alert to indicate the event has been triggered.
